GT Equivalence Verification (PO36)

GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*exp(-Abs(x))*v
Candidates evaluated: 50

Matched candidates: ["c0*x + c1 + c2*v*exp(c3*x) + c4*exp(c5*x)*sin(c6*t + c7)"]

I need to determine which candidates can exactly match the Ground Truth:

**GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*exp(-|x|)*v = 0.156063*sin(t) - 0.372948*v*exp(-x)**

Since x > 0 on this domain, |x| = x, so GT = 0.156063*sin(t) - 0.372948*v*exp(-x).

The GT has two terms:
1. A sin(t) term
2. A v*exp(-x) term

Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce exactly these basis functions.

**Candidate 1:** c0*x + c1 + c2*v + c3*v + c4*v³ + c5*sin(c6*t+c7) + c8*v³ + c9*v*x²
Set c0=c1=0, c4=c8=0, c9=0. Left with (c2+c3)*v + c5*sin(c6*t+c7). This gives linear v, not v*exp(-x). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** c0*x + c1 + c2*v*x² + c3*v + c4*v³ + c5*v + c6*exp(c7*x)*sin(c8*t+c9)
Set c0=c1=c2=c4=0. Left with (c3+c5)*v + c6*exp(c7*x)*sin(c8*t+c9). The v term is not v*exp(-x), and the sin term is coupled with exp. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** Polynomial + sin + v³ + v*x² + rational. No v*exp(-x). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** c0*x + c1 + c2*x^c3*exp(c4*v) + c5*exp(c6*x)*sin(c7*t+c8). The exp(c4*v) term can't give v*exp(-x). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 11:** c0*x + c1 + c2*v + c3*v³ + c4*sin(c5*t+c6). Set c0=c1=c3=0: c2*v + c4*sin(c5*t+c6). This is linear in v, not v*exp(-x). **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 12-28:** Similar analysis - none have v*exp(-x) as a basis function. They have v, v³, v*Abs(v), etc.

**Candidate 29:** c0*x + c1 + c2*v*exp(c3*x) + c4*exp(c5*x)*sin(c6*t+c7). Set c0=c1=0, c3=-1, c5=0: c2*v*exp(-x) + c4*sin(c6*t+c7). This matches GT! Set c2=-0.372948, c4=0.156063, c6=1, c7=0. **MATCH**
